- SCROLL-TO-TOP ON CLIENT SWITCH — the Shell remount (LORAMER_SHELL_CLIENT_CONTEXT_V1) leaves the user MID-PAGE: switching clients keeps the prior scroll position instead of landing at the top. Observed by Russ on Team, mobile, during Gate-B. The remount is correct and stays; this is the missing companion — a client switch should land at the top of the page. Small, -next only, rides the next UI flight. src: Russ Gate-B 2026-07-16. open [LC]
- HOMEPAGE UNIFICATION — **NOW ON THE CRITICAL PATH of the only external launch gate** (was a standing pre-launch item). loramer.com marketing ↔ app.loramer.com landing; Sign-in-with-Google lives ONLY on the app. Raised explicitly by Russ 2026-07-16 while fixing the Google OAuth branding rejection: the consent screen's Application home page points at loramer.com, so that page's content is now a REVIEW SURFACE, not just marketing — every copy decision there is a launch-gate decision until verification clears. src: Russ 2026-07-16. open [LC]
- ★ G2.7 — THE TAIL (rank past topN) — **POST-LAUNCH.** Lora can RANK but not REACH past topN (clamp [1,50], no offset); for search_term the rows are already in lambda memory and discarded. TWO ASKS, DIFFERENT SHAPES: · FILTER (the real build) — "what's wasting money" = spend>0 AND conversions=0, ranked; RANK-INDEPENDENT (the biggest waste is often #1 — Escential's "essential oils" $155 / 34 clicks / 0 conv sits at the top), no paging needed. · OFFSET (cheap, rides along) — LIMIT/OFFSET on the bounded path, array slice on the unbounded path. ⚠ VOLUME FLOOR REQUIRED: zero-conversions catches dead terms AND terms with 2 clicks that never had a chance — naming those is confidently-wrong advice, same class as the Display hour-0 midnight bid-down. Floor threshold is Russ's call, unset. READ-ONLY OUTPUT: Lora RECOMMENDS the negative-keyword list, the user pastes it into Google — no write scopes, NOT blocked by the 2027 write destination. src: 2026-07-16. open [LC]
- ★ G2.5 — GEO ABSENCE DIAGNOSIS ("where am I blind?") — **POST-LAUNCH, ordered AFTER ★G2.** WHY: Lora can say what happened somewhere; she CANNOT say where NOTHING happened. Absence is never served by any platform — Google returns zero rows for zero-activity geos (banked 2026-06-28; NOT a false-zero bug, correct behavior). Absence must therefore be COMPUTED at question-time: targeted universe MINUS observed rows.
- ★ G2.6 — DENOMINATOR LAYER (cross-cutting normalization; NOT a geo feature) — **POST-LAUNCH, ordered AFTER ★G2; does NOT gate G2 or G2.5.** WHY — THE MOAT CASE: GA says Wyoming sends high organic traffic; Google says zero impressions there. "Demand exists and you are not buying it" is multi-source-provenance law at its sharpest — the value is explaining WHY sources disagree, and presence-vs-absence is the sharpest disagreement. Same shape for Shopify conversion rate by state, GA sessions, Google impressions. Any geo dimension can borrow it.
- ★ G2.8 — GEO CARD PARAMS — **UI WIRING, not data layer.** The card-breakdown route (src/app/api/next/card-breakdown/route.ts) does not forward geoGrain/geoScope to queryBreakdown, so the collapsed geo grains (city/metro/postal/county/state/province/district/most_specific, ad|user) can't be requested through the card route — a 'geo' card returns the "geo needs geoGrain" note, no rows. geo_country/geo_region cards name places TODAY (own tool types, no grain needed) and already carry geoName end-to-end (LORAMER_GEO_RESOLVER_V1). FIX: add geoGrain/geoScope passthrough on the card route (the route's own "dep #2 expands it" surface). src: 2026-07-16. open [LC]
- ★ G2.9 — DMA SUPPLEMENT — closes the last ~0.41% of geo coverage. ~210 US DMAs via Google's GeoTargetConstant API (the metro/DMA grain is 100% unresolvable from the zero-quota CSV — banked DECISION "NO METRO/DMA IN THE CSV"). Small run (~210 lookups), quota-gated: Basic Access 15k ops/day, exhausts ~11:42 UTC, blocked until ~08:03 UTC → run in the MORNING window. UPSERTs into geo_target_constant (accumulates, same table). Metro rows resolve to names after. src: 2026-07-16. open [LC]
- ★ GEO LOADER RE-RUN CADENCE — the geotargets CSV is revised roughly ANNUALLY. scripts/ingest-geo-target-constants.mjs is IDEMPOTENT (a re-run of the same version changes 0 rows; a new version UPSERTs new/changed ids, retires-but-keeps dropped ones — RETENTION LAW). WHERE TO SCHEDULE: a low-frequency cron (e.g. monthly is ample; it self-detects the newest published version and no-ops if unchanged) — NOT scheduled in this commit; wire it when the cron surface is next touched. src: 2026-07-16. open [LC]
- ★ EVAL-BIND — tests/lora-evals/golden-set.json references "Influential Drones" BY NAME. TWO clients carry that name (see DECISIONS "TWO CLIENTS ARE NAMED Influential Drones"). The rubric numbers (Shopify $128,896.56, GA $13,609.20) match ONLY the real 5bb9b2ff — the demo fixture 2617b163 has NO Shopify and NO GA connection at all. If the harness binds by name it can grade a client that LACKS the very data being graded — the 2026-06-23 wrong-copy failure mode living inside Lora's launch gate. VERIFY how run-evals.mjs resolves the client; PIN it to the id (5bb9b2ff), not the name. src: 2026-07-16 verify. open [LC]
- ★ LEGACY-PIN vs -NEXT CUTOVER — isLegacyCohort (src/lib/legacy-cohort.ts:9) pins demo@loramer.com, shopify-reviewer@loramer.app, and shopify+*@loramer.app to the LEGACY surface, enforced in BOTH middleware.ts:33 (Edge) AND preview-gate.ts (Node). Correct WHILE legacy = the screencast UI. But when -next becomes the DEFAULT surface (queued cutover), these fixtures stay pinned to legacy PERMANENTLY — including the Shopify reviewer, whose credential obligation (DECISIONS "REVIEWER-TOKEN LOGIN…") requires access to the app's COMPLETE feature set. If the complete feature set lives on -next post-cutover, a reviewer pinned to legacy may not see it. DECIDE before the cutover, not after — Russ's call; it turns on what Shopify's listing binds. src: 2026-07-16 verify. open [LC]
- ★ UI-OVERFLOW (Bug 1) — **OPEN. NOT FIXED.** Four theories proposed, all four WRONG; two fixes shipped to prod (25b4957, 78de5ab), NEITHER resolved it. Unchanged on device as of 2026-07-16 23:26 (Russ, iPhone 17 Pro Max, BOTH Chrome and Safari — not engine-specific; not worse than before). SYMPTOM: Ask Lora on a client page → send a query returning a WIDE TABLE → the sheet pans horizontally, the send arrow ends up off the right edge, and with the keyboard up the dashboard beneath (chart lines, axis labels, "Change account", the ROAS rules box) is visible under/around the sheet (Safari shows less than Chrome; both show it).
- ★ LEGACY-CHAT-OVERFLOW — src/app/dashboard/page.tsx ALSO renders ReactMarkdown with its OWN styling and does NOT import chat.module.css, so it carries the SAME latent wide-table + code-block overflow; the LORAMER_NEXT_CHAT_FLEX_MINWIDTH_V1 fix does NOT reach it. That surface is where isLegacyCohort pins demo@ and shopify-reviewer@ — and the Shopify reviewer credential obligation requires access to the app's COMPLETE feature set, so a broken chat there is not cosmetic. FIX: same shape (min-width:0 on its flex chain + table/pre scrollers) applied to page.tsx's own markdown styles. Cross-ref ★LEGACY-PIN vs -NEXT CUTOVER. src: 2026-07-16. open [LC]
- ★ CHAT-GATE-ZINDEX — ClientPage.tsx:408's value-model gate is position:fixed; inset:0; z-index:1000, ABOVE the chat's z-index:60. On any client with an UNSET value model, opening Ask Lora renders the gate ("Set this client's value model to continue" / "Save & continue") OVER the chat. Escential HAS a value model, which is why Russ hit the keyboard page-bleed instead of this. NOT fixed by LORAMER_NEXT_CHAT_VISUAL_VIEWPORT_V1 — different cause (stacking, not keyboard). DECIDE which surface owns the top of the stack (cap the gate below the chat, or block the chat while the gate is up). src: 2026-07-16 UI recon. open [LC]
- ★ MOBILE-WIDTH-GUARD — a guard to catch mobile horizontal-overflow regressions (the chat-arrow class). CAVEAT THIS FLIGHT PROVED (load-bearing): a headless RENDER-MEASUREMENT guard PASSES while the bug is live on iOS — Playwright WebKit contained a 976px table at 390px BEFORE the fix. If built, it MUST assert the CSS INVARIANT (min-width:0 present on the flex chain; overflow-x:auto on .md table and .md pre) OR run on a real iOS surface. A width-measurement guard would have shipped this bug GREEN (DECISIONS "HEADLESS CANNOT SEE THE iOS FLEX BUG"). src: 2026-07-16. open [LC]
- ★ DEPLOY-WEBHOOK — **RESOLVED (transient); STAYS OPEN pending recurrence.** WHAT HAPPENED (history, keep it): 2026-07-16 ~21:10Z git-push deployment CREATION silently stopped — commits be58a07 and 9b14d16 pushed cleanly to origin/main but Vercel created NO deployment record in ANY state (not canceled, not errored, not queued; 543d315 at 21:10:45Z was the last git-created deploy, READY). RESOLUTION: **NOT broken — a transient webhook delivery/processing failure.** Vercel support confirmed from their side: no deployment records existed for be58a07/9b14d16, project config was correct throughout (gitProviderOptions.createDeployments enabled, production branch main, no git.deploymentEnabled:false), and git deploys resumed after the CLI deploy. CONFIRMED BY OBSERVATION (commit 25b4957): the deploy was created BY THE GIT INTEGRATION (source=git) — the trigger works; Vercel also FLUSHED THE BACKLOG (be58a07, 9b14d16, ac5e6b9, a06d68e each got their own git-created deployment, all READY). So it was a DELAYED webhook queue that recovered, not a permanent break. **NO manual CLI step is required going forward.** The one-time CLI deploy (dpl_HqiUCbJhr4fZ9D4S7cEKD7AnNdUh, 9b14d16 tree) was the unblock, not a standing workaround. STAYS OPEN: watch the next several commits — a one-off delay and a systemic fault look identical from inside one incident. If it recurs, the Vercel case is open with the SHAs (be58a07, 9b14d16) + the 2026-07-16T21:10:45Z boundary. THE LAW STANDS REGARDLESS: DECISIONS "A PUSH IS NOT A DEPLOY" — every local gate read green while prod served old code and nothing in the pipeline noticed; confirm a deployment EXISTS and reads READY against the expected commit before handing Russ any Gate-B check. src: 2026-07-16 deploy-integration diagnosis + Vercel support. open-watch [LC]
- ★ SUPPORT-BOT — **POST-LAUNCH, NOT before 2026-07-22.** THE MODEL (Vercel's support bot, 2026-07-16): it answered "what happened to MY project" by reading Russ's ACTUAL deployment history, his createDeployments flag, his production branch — not documentation. It confirmed our diagnosis independently, named PRECISELY where its access ended (webhook delivery logs are not self-service), offered a human, then drafted the support case PRE-FILLED with everything it already knew — leaving Russ only the two things it could NOT infer: which project + the deployment URL. THE LESSON: ask ONLY what you cannot look up; every support form that makes a user retype what the system already knows is a form that never read its own database. SCOPE — SMALLER THAN LORA, NOT BIGGER: Lora does open-ended analysis over millions of rows across five platforms and explains why sources disagree; a support bot answers a narrow, mostly-CLOSED set — is my connection healthy, why is my data missing, when did my backfill last run, why is this number different from the platform's. Those are LOOKUPS against state that already exists: platform_connections.health / last_ok_at / last_error_code, sync_state cursors + backfill_complete, the __google_quota sentinel, cron_runs. Same architectural shape as query_metrics (tools over the DB, scoped to the caller); different tables, different skill doc — the hard part is already built. TWO/THREE THINGS THAT DECIDE GOOD vs LIABILITY: (1) SCOPING IS THE WHOLE GAME — Vercel's bot saw Russ's project and ONLY Russ's project; a LoraMer support bot reading connection health must be ORG-SCOPED AT THE TOOL LAYER, not by prompt. The org spine exists (RBAC, migration 027 org_id NOT-NULL) but this is the FIRST tool that reads PLUMBING rather than metrics — treat it as a new RBAC surface, not a new prompt. (2) IT MUST SAY "I DON'T KNOW" — name the exact edge of its access and hand off; a bot that invents a cause for a broken connection is WORSE than no bot (the user acts on it). Same law as LORA_SPEC's settled-vs-contested calibration: confident wrongness is the liability. (3) ESCALATION SHAPE — when it cannot answer, draft the ticket PRE-FILLED and ask only for what it cannot infer; LoraMer's analogue of Vercel's "deployment URL" is which client / which date range / which platform — everything else (connection health, cursor position, last sync, quota state) it already has. src: 2026-07-16 Vercel support-bot model. open [LC]
- ★ CLIENT-BIO — agency-facing client biographical/contact block (NOT Lora). WHAT: an editable block on the client profile page — client NAME (editable), contact person, phone, email, and whatever else the shape suggests. For the AGENCY's use, not Lora's. Russ's immediate itch: "Veterinary mastermind" (f5fbe7e5) should be "Veterinary Mastermind" and there is no way to fix it today. **THREE THINGS THE RECON MUST ANSWER BEFORE ANY BUILD — do not skip to the form:** (1) THE NAME HAZARD (load-bearing) — ★EVAL-BIND is already banked: tests/lora-evals/golden-set.json references "Influential Drones" BY NAME and TWO clients carry that name (5bb9b2ff real, 2617b163 demo@ fixture). Free renaming means anything resolving by name silently points elsewhere. Whether anything BESIDES the eval harness binds by name is UNVERIFIED — grep EVERYTHING (code, scripts, tests, fixtures, evals, docs, cron, seeds) before allowing an editable name field. Also: is client name UNIQUE-constrained? Two clients already share a name, so it is NOT. If the answer is "nothing breaks", say so plainly — cautious-for-no-reason is its own failure. (2) PII — contact person / phone / email is personal data about THIRD PARTIES (the agency's clients' staff, people who never signed up for LoraMer) — a different category from client business data. VERIFY whether the app stores any third-party PII today; if it does NOT, this is a first, and the privacy policy must say we store it BEFORE we store it. The privacy policy is already on the Google OAuth critical path — NOT a blocker, a SEQUENCING constraint. (3) RBAC — who can edit? Owner / Admin / Member. Banked open item: Team Management V2 carries an unresolved "admin-vs-owner permission decision" — determine whether contact-edit DEPENDS on that decision or is orthogonal. **ALSO CHECK:** whether the banked 2026-06-05 "Additional Context box + Industry selector" roadmap item overlaps this — it may be the SAME surface, and building two bio boxes on one page is the "build it twice" trap. BLAST RADIUS WHEN BUILT: schema (new columns on clients) + client profile UI + an edit path where one may not exist. src: Russ 2026-07-16. NOT STARTED. open [LC]
- ★ WHOLE-SURFACE UI BEHAVIOR AUDIT — **OWED AND UNSCHEDULED. THE OPEN BLIND SPOT.** The 2026-07-15 master audit covered CAPTURE and LORA. **It never covered the UI.** Every UI bug found on 2026-07-15/16 — the team wrong-client (Ask-Lora answering about Ennis while the URL said Veterinary, PROVEN in prod), the client-profile state bleed (NaicsPicker query/selected/touched + ClientPage gateDraft pre-ticking the previous client's value-model answers), the readiness checklist not reflecting saved state, the scroll-to-top regression — **came from RUSS CLICKING, not from any instrument.** No audit, no eval, no guard was looking at the UI; the 28/28 eval doesn't touch it and the 2026-07-11 parity audit asked EXISTS/PARTIAL/MISSING (an INVENTORY question, which cannot answer a CORRECTNESS question — banked as law). What is owed: a whole-surface UI BEHAVIOR audit using the SAME method that found G1 — enumerate every -next surface × every state carrier × every write path, derive truth from the code and the live DB, and state plainly what the audit CANNOT see. Until it runs, the honest posture is: **the UI is unaudited, and the only detector we have is Russ.** src: 2026-07-16. open [LC]
- ★ SOURCE-CONFLICT-GATE — build-resume-digest.mjs (or a sibling script) should detect CONTRADICTIONS BETWEEN gated source docs, not just hash them. The freshness gate today is a CONSISTENCY check (digest matches its sources), not a TRUTH check (sources agree with each other) — which is why 2026-07-17 opened with a stale RUSS ACTION #1 pointing at a Google OAuth gate closed the day before, with all 10 hashes green (see DECISIONS LORAMER_SOURCE_CONFLICT_GATE_V1). MINIMUM VIABLE: grep for terms banked as CLOSED/RETIRED/APPROVED in DECISIONS and FAIL if another gated doc still asserts them open/pending. ★ MUST ALSO (added 2026-07-17, the G2 lesson): verify that CONTINUE_HERE §E's NAMED next-item still reads OPEN in the QUEUE — "next" is authored (not derivable: no priority field, ordering is Russ's judgment), so a contradiction check is the only guard, and that single check would have caught "NEXT BUILD = G2" the moment G2's QUEUE line flipped to done [LC]. This is the post-launch completion of LORAMER_DOCS_SINGLE_OWNER_V1 (the deletion half shipped 2026-07-17): the board (one structured status source) + generated-§E-status + this gate together make the ~10 volatile facts impossible-to-drift rather than merely deleted. NOT BUILT — banking the SHAPE only; do NOT build now (5 days from launch, and it adds a generated surface). src: 2026-07-17. open [NP]
- ★ DERIVE-INVENTORY-FROM-WRITERS — docs/LORAMER_DEFINITIVE_CAPTURE_INVENTORY.md was RETIRED from the gated set 2026-07-17 (LORAMER_DOCS_SINGLE_OWNER_V1) because it is a hand-maintained map that admits it is stale (pre-dates 6 shipped writers; "a map can rot silently while every hash stays green"). It stays TRACKED + in place so the ~10 live §6 gap-list references do not dangle, but it is ARCHIVAL, not current. THE FIX (same shape as REGISTRY→claude-tools generation): GENERATE the capture surface map + §6 cross-platform gap list FROM the writers + live DISTINCT (platform, breakdown_type, entity_level) rows, so it cannot drift from code. Until then, the live gap-truth is the writers + docs/LORAMER_DATA_COMPLETENESS.md. Cross-ref ★MAP-vs-CODE DRIFT (same generate-don't-guard principle for BREAKDOWN_REGISTRY §2). src: 2026-07-17. open [NP]
- ★ DOC-OWNERSHIP-GUARD — the MECHANICAL version of CLAUDE.md's DOC-OWNERSHIP GATES (LORAMER_CLAUDE_MD_DOC_GATES_V1): a build-enforced script (check-doc-ownership.mjs) that reads the OWNERSHIP MAP in CLAUDE.md, greps the facts each doc is declared to OWN, and FAILS the build if another gated doc asserts them in the PRESENT TENSE (dated log entries = tense-locked history, allowed; present-tense assertions = copies, fail). The refusal gates in CLAUDE.md bind Claude Code (strong, but talk-out-of-able); this binds the compiler (cannot be talked out of it) — the real fix, per the FIX-WITH-GUARD + RULE-HOME laws. ⚠ HONEST HARD PART (state it, do not fake it): "present-tense assertion of an owned fact" is not a trivial grep — it needs the owned-fact list to be machine-readable (the CLAUDE.md ownership map is prose today) and a tense/context heuristic that does not false-fail on pointers or pedagogical reference-with-context. Likely ONE build with ★SOURCE-CONFLICT-GATE (that one checks DECISIONS CLOSED/APPROVED terms vs other docs + §E's named next-item vs the QUEUE; this one checks the broader owned-fact map) — same script, same grep-owned-facts-then-fail shape. POST-LAUNCH; do NOT build now. src: 2026-07-17. open [NP]
- ★ INSIGHT-INVESTIGATOR — the insight bar is a REBUILD, not a model swap (post ★OPUS-EVERYWHERE; deliberate speed, behind the 07-16 unfinished work). Roadmapped 2026-06-10 as the While-You-Were-Sleeping digest: every metric with meaningful overnight movement, each with a specific recommendation + a connecting overall-strategy explanation. Russ 07-17: it must answer WHY — not "you spent more last night" but "because <search term> ate $X" or "a spike from <city>, TX." THAT IS A TOOL LOOP, not a completion: detect → drill (query_metrics then query_breakdown, iteratively — the same loop chat runs on a "why" question). Haiku cannot drive a tool loop — the real reason the model decision was never a blurb-quality question. ONLY POSSIBLE SINCE 2026-07-16: until G2 closed, Lora could not reach geo / GA dimensional / age_gender — the "why" data was captured and UNREADABLE; now 118/118. THREE DESIGN CONSTRAINTS, each a way this ships BROKEN: (1) ATTRIBUTION IS NOT SHARE — the anomaly is a delta against ITS OWN baseline, not its share of the total; naive top-N names the biggest line item every night and trains users to ignore the bar. (2) A CAPTURE HOLE LOOKS EXACTLY LIKE A COLLAPSE — G1 froze Meta breadth 17 days; a detector running then would have screamed "conversions dropped to zero" every morning (false-zero law on the most-read surface in the app); the detector MUST distinguish NO DATA from ZERO → it needs reconcile/capture state, not just metrics. (3) SPLIT THE MATH FROM THE PROSE — detection is deterministic (thresholds, baselines, code); Lora EXPLAINS what the math found (preserves the determinism law; stops the model DECIDING what is anomalous, which is where hallucinated urgency comes from). ⚠ COST STOPS BEING TRIVIAL HERE — but of the DESTINATION, not today: when built this becomes a multi-turn investigation per client per day = the highest-frequency call in the product AT THE DESTINATION (N clients daily); the CURRENT insight call is near-ZERO (legacy-cohort only, below). Model the cost BEFORE building. ⚠ CORRECTED 2026-07-17 — THIS IS A BUILD, NOT AN UPGRADE TO A LIVE SURFACE: the proactive insight surface DOES NOT EXIST on -next (MultiClientOverview.tsx:184 is a neutral "Proactive insights … coming soon" placeholder; the real banner lives ONLY in the legacy dashboard, page.tsx:1415/:1523, and middleware.ts:33-38 redirects every non-legacy-cohort user away from it — VERIFIED; anthropic_spend_log last-7-days had ZERO organic insight calls, only a Shopify reviewer fixture). So ★INSIGHT-INVESTIGATOR = build the -next banner ITSELF + the precompute engine + the schedule, from the placeholder up — not an upgrade to a running surface. The Opus floor (★OPUS-EVERYWHERE) is already correct and waiting for it. src: roadmap 2026-06-10 + Russ 2026-07-17. open [LC]
- ★ DIGEST-WINDOW-MODEL — the SETTLED shape (Russ 2026-07-17) for the While-You-Were-Sleeping digest's WINDOW + SCHEDULING. · TIMEZONE IS A PROPERTY OF THE CLIENT: "while THEY slept" = their overnight on THEIR clock; a Pacific client's window is Pacific even when the agency is Eastern. · THE SCHEDULE IS A PROPERTY OF THE READER: the agency opens the app at THEIR 6am and everything computed so far is sitting there — NO per-client-morning fan-out scheduler is needed; each window computes on its own clock and surfaces whenever the reader looks. A Pacific client's 7pm-7am ends at 10am ET, so it is NOT ready at 6am ET — a fact about the earth, not a bug; Lora STATES it ("Pacific clients through 7am PT, ready ~10am ET") per the honesty law. · THE WINDOW IS DIRECTABLE: default 7pm-7am local, overridable per client, with an agency-level default new clients inherit — a settings field + a client-profile field, NOT new architecture. · WHAT EXISTS (VERIFIED 2026-07-17): organizations carries only (id, name, owner_email, org_type, created_at) — no timezone, no logo, no settings PAGE anywhere; client_context IS the business-context page already (ClientPage.tsx → /api/context); NO timezone column in ANY table. · TIMEZONE IS DERIVABLE, NOT ASKABLE, FOR MOST: google-ads.ts:26,35 ALREADY fetches customer_client.time_zone into the live intelligence and throws it away; Shopify exposes shop.iana_timezone and we never ask; Meta uses advertiser TZ for hour buckets and we store the label, not the zone. Derive first; the settings page is the human override. · THE INTERPRETATION JOB, not the scheduling job: platform hours are reported in the ACCOUNT's timezone — a Pacific client's "22:00" is the agency's 01:00; converting platform hours to the client's real clock is what makes an overnight window MEAN anything (that is why the account timezone matters — NOT for firing a cron). · CARDINALITY (Russ's model confirmed, mine corrected): ONE org + N client_contexts for BOTH agency and owner; nothing constrains an owner to one client (one 'business' account already has two) — same shape, different convention, NOT two page types. src: Russ 2026-07-17. open [LC]
- ★ HOUR-GRAIN-CAPTURE-HOLE — launch-relevant; VIOLATES ESSENCE (capture everything, FULL GRAIN). VERIFIED 2026-07-17: Google + Meta store hour grain; Shopify, WooCommerce, and GA DO NOT — and it is OUR choice, not a platform limit. Shopify's Admin API returns order createdAt to the SECOND; our writer aggregates to a daily row and DISCARDS the timestamp. Woo the same. GA4 exposes an hour dimension; we capture 12 GA dimensional types and NONE is hourly. ⇒ "Someone ordered at 3am" — the single most interesting sentence an overnight digest could say — is UNANSWERABLE because we threw the timestamp away. A direct violation of CAPTURE EVERYTHING / FULL GRAIN. THREE WRITERS, not three platforms (Shopify + Woo + GA hour capture). src: 2026-07-17 verify. open [LC]
- ★ PLATFORM-SURFACE-AUDIT — for EACH of the five platforms, enumerate FROM THE PLATFORM'S OWN DOCS every field, dimension, and grain the API OFFERS; diff against what metrics_daily holds; report the delta. Reference = the VENDOR'S docs, NEVER our writers/inventory/registry (see DECISIONS "EVERY AUDIT SO FAR COMPARED US TO OURSELVES"). This is the audit the other three should have been: the capture audits + the 2026-07-11 parity audit compared us to ourselves; G2 (07-16) found 118 captured-but-UNREADABLE tuples (the READ side) — this checks the WRITE side (offered-but-never-fetched, e.g. the hour-grain hole above). Sized honestly: five platforms, real work. src: 2026-07-17. open [LC] — GOOGLE ADS SECTION = ✅ COMPLETE (vendor-sourced 2026-07-18; result → docs/LORAMER_DATA_COMPLETENESS.md "## GOOGLE ADS — PLATFORM-SURFACE-AUDIT RESULT"). Meta / Shopify / Woo / GA4 = STILL TO DIFF (item stays open until all five done). GOOGLE CAPTURE-COMPLETION BUILD QUEUE (ranked; each [LC]; each still gated by Gate-A + adapter-gate real-API validation before any writer ships):
- ★ CLAUDE-MD-COPIES — the copied code-facts enumerated 2026-07-17 (LORAMER_CLAUDE_MD_MODEL_POINTER_V1 already pointed the model IDs; these remain). FIX THE TWO ALREADY-WRONG FIRST: (a) the Supabase table LIST in CLAUDE.md asserts 9 tables and is missing 13+ that exist NOW (organizations, org_members, org_client_grants, known_floors, geo_target_constant, woo_connect_nonce, anthropic_spend_log, dashboard_layouts, user_profiles, uploaded_docs, sync_state, cron_runs, woocommerce_tokens) — a map of the database wrong by more than half, in the file the executor reads EVERY session; POINT at the schema (migrations/ + list_tables), do not list tables. (b) "dashboard/page.tsx — 3000+ lines" is understated (the file is ~4197); drop the number. The OTHER EIGHT are correct-today copies (same disease, lower velocity), each → a pointer or dropped: 16k max_tokens, Google Ads API v23, Shopify GraphQL '2025-01', Next.js 14, localhost:3000, the ~15min intelligence-cache TTL, the advar- localStorage prefix, the platform type union 'google'|'meta'|'combined'. Cross-ref ★DOC-OWNERSHIP-GUARD (the mechanical enforcer that would fail the build on the present-tense copies). src: 2026-07-17 CLAUDE.md audit. open [NP]

## I. LESSONS INDEX 1–60 (+ dated)  (source: LORAMER_DECISIONS.md)
1 Silent-skip via shared marker — use content-based idempotency, not marker-presence.
2 Scope assumption in destructure adds — grep the prop in the parent's scope before patching.
3 TS prop add = two edits/component (destructure AND type; check inline vs multi-line type).
4 JS string apostrophes break builds — use backticks for any string with apostrophes/quotes.
5 Stale anchors — re-read the current file (fresh sed/grep) before any patch.
6 Marker-collision silent failure — distinct sub-markers OR per-edit content checks.
7 Per-edit content-based idempotency check is the best practice (all/some/none present logic).
8 Silent .catch(()=>[]) hides GAQL/API errors — instrument console.error before concluding "no data".
9 Cache invalidation hides deployed fixes (15-min) — force a miss via a never-used date range.
10 Whitespace in anchors — bytes matter; dump exact bytes when an anchor fails.
11 PROMPT-AS-MIRROR — grounding/constraint text goes in code comments (INTERNAL_GROUNDING), never user-rendered prompt.
12 Meta breakdowns go in &breakdowns=, NOT &fields= (else HTTP 400, swallowed by .catch).
13 Same-line comment after a token (comma/paren/bracket/template) can break webpack — comment on its own line.
14 tsc --noEmit is NOT npm run build — webpack is stricter (syntax/mangled-literals); build is the real gate.
15 Surfacing raw API status/body into the prompt = diagnostic of last resort (always with a planned cleanup).
16 Anchor only from the current-turn paste — never memory/earlier turns/grep; small anchors over big.
17 Same-named files + blind mv is dangerous — unique-name downloads before moving.
18 Patch scripts with hardcoded machine paths silently fail — match the machine's path.
19 ONE canonical date resolver (resolveDateWindow) — never roll per-platform date math.
20 Revenue = NET (currentSubtotalPriceSet), not gross — surface refunds; match merchant analytics.
21 GAQL has NO LAST_90_DAYS enum — explicit BETWEEN via resolveDateWindow.
22 Platform selector and tab nav are separate controls — switch to Overview on platform change from a non-ad tab.
23 Safe Supabase dup cleanup — backup→repoint children→verify counts→delete only emptied twins (keeper isn't always older).
24 Bug hunts in big files — investigate-only first, then a tight fix spec.
25 Repo is single source of truth — git pull at session start on either machine; unpushed work doesn't travel.
26a Serverless backfill cross-request cursor race — do the whole job in ONE invocation (in-memory loop); persist the cursor only for resume-after-interrupt, never as the loop's control.
26b RightPanel renders TWIN desktop/mobile message containers (hidden md:flex / flex md:hidden, both in DOM) — audit BOTH when touching either; assign anchors by document order. (HANDOFF dual-numbered both as "26"; HANDOFF:730 explicitly notes the collision.)
27 zsh eats unquoted globs (quote --include="*.ts"); BSD grep needs -E for alternation.
28 Verify a freshly-deployed cron/route against LIVE prod + give it time (stale triggers/logs mislead).
29 Heredoc/terminal pastes drop characters — deliver code as files; tsc catches mangled identifiers, NOT mangled string literals — grep critical strings.
30 Backfill depth = "as deep as the platform serves," discovered by probing; report the ACTUAL earliest row, never the swept cursor.
31 Per-platform retention differs — probe before trusting any documented limit.
32 JSX comments are {/* */}, not /* */ (renders as visible text; tsc misses it).
33 CRON-GATED VERIFICATION — deploy before the cron window or manually trigger after; capture writes YESTERDAY's date.
34 Handoffs anchor on session TAG + files, never a commit hash (local commits squash/rewrite on push).
35 pg_dump in CI: invoke by ABSOLUTE path /usr/lib/postgresql/17/bin/pg_dump (PATH resolves to v16).
36 GitHub Actions "Re-run jobs" replays the ORIGINAL commit — use a fresh workflow_dispatch to test a fix.
37 Vercel env rotation needs a redeploy to bind; native cron rotates atomically with the redeploy.
38 Supabase DB password is reset-safe (app uses API keys, not raw Postgres password).
39 A DB write that must touch a row → UPSERT (not UPDATE) + check affected count, log loudly on 0; never assume success on no-throw.
40 Never render internal flag/enum/status/tier keys to users — pass through a human-label map next to the keys.
41 Stripe Portal "cancel at period end" sets cancel_at (timestamp), not cancel_at_period_end (boolean).
42 Google OAuth consent-screen edits (name/domains/scopes/URLs/logo) trigger RE-verification — treat as frozen at launch.
43 Google Ads permissible-use update → Tool Change Form (zero-risk MCC metadata), not a full Standard Access app.
44 Walk every onboarding identity SHAPE with a real identity before launch (founder-only testing only exercises one shape).
45 vercel env pull can report a populated prod var as blank — verify "empty env" against runtime behavior; never re-set to a guess.
46 An API probe verifies what the CREDENTIAL can see, not what EXISTS — a boundary coinciding with a known limit IS the explanation; scope-truncated $0 rows are false-zeros, delete them.
47 EVERYTHING GETS EVERYTHING — completeness is a CORRECTNESS requirement; every gap explicit; any cap is a logged deliberate decision (MATRIX).
48 Vercel MCP has NO env-write — rotate via CLI (value via stdin, never printed) + redeploy to bind.
49 Guard NOT-NULL numerics vs NaN at the WRITE BOUNDARY (Number.isFinite), not per-builder (NaN ?? 0 = NaN → 23502 drops the whole row).
50 Don't conclude a logic bug from a symptom seen under one timing — replay the exact query against live DB; schedule catchup AFTER forward.
51 A backfill DRIVER LOOP must circuit-break on a persistent per-window error; never oscillate/re-walk; be gentle on live stores; resume from the TRUE frontier; when in doubt, STOP and surface.
52 Next.js App Router caches global fetch → deterministic supabase-js reads/writes go STALE/DROPPED on Vercel; force-no-store on read-after-write routes; a unique request body masks the bug.
53 A persisted UI selection carried across a context switch must be RE-VALIDATED against the new context (derive caps from the incoming entity); land on a valid non-blank default.
54 Shopify managed-install scopes come from the DEPLOYED config (shopify app deploy), not the authorize-URL scope= param; a refresh preserves the original grant; verify a scope change by PROBE.
55 A flag-gated reconnect control can be invisible exactly when needed — any re-auth/extend-scope affordance must be reachable for a HEALTHY connection.
56 shopify app deploy needs the Shopify CLI on node ≥22.12 (CLI 4.x crashes on node 20).
57 Vercel env VALUES are unreadable from tooling (masked / pull-blanked / no MCP env tool) — confirm from the source system.
58 Shopify revenue basis differs BY GRAIN — reconcile to the cent (per-line refund attribution + pro-rata residual) or ship a silent per-SKU lie; a WRONG basis is worse than no basis.
59 A permanent-history backfill must self-reconcile per unit of work (Σ within 1¢ each day BEFORE write/cursor-advance) or HALT loudly — never persist a bad day.
60 A connection-state claim (broken/dead/frozen/blocked/unhealthy/reconnect-needed) is a HYPOTHESIS until a LIVE capture-path probe proves it — never written as fact from a stored flag (health/last_error_code/oauth_190/last_ok_at) alone; stored flags are DERIVED CONTEXT, not ground truth (same class as the Google end_date adapter-semantics bug). Origin: a prior session wrote "Influential Drones Meta BLOCKED/broken/oauth_190" into CONTINUE_HERE + QUEUE + a session log as settled fact from the flag alone — it was FALSE (token alive HTTP 200, warehouse reconciled to the penny) and survived days because each session read it forward without re-deriving. RULE: before writing any negative connection claim into ANY handoff doc, run a live probe (raw HTTP status + body, Lesson 15 style); until probed, record "flag says X — UNVERIFIED, probe before acting," never as a blocker. The transient-190-dark-flags-a-live-connection generator = WS2 #2 (separate fix).
61 A backfill writer must STOP AT its retention floor as an EMPTY SUCCESS (per-adapter granularMonths clamp — meta=36, GA fixed 2015-08-14, Google account/dim 132mo), NOT overshoot into a boundary THROW; a step is 'done' ONLY on empty-success-at-floor or reconciled-to-floor, NEVER on an error. Origin: the onboarding drain's Meta account step stoppedOnError at the ~37mo boundary (it overshot to 132mo), never completed, and BLOCKED the later placement step. Fix (LORAMER_ONBOARD_DRAIN_V1): granularMonths=36 for meta; PER-STEP-INDEPENDENT drain (a stuck early step never starves a later one); verified Meta taxonomy decides done-vs-retry-vs-surface ({1,2,4,17,613,80004}/429/timeout=retry · 100·1487534=narrow-the-window · 100-other/190/368=surface · empty-success=done); NEVER swallow the fetch error (L15) — surface code/subcode so floor-vs-transient is distinguishable.
62 A platform-wide "stall" + a cluster of serverless TIMEOUTS with NO DB/lock/deadlock evidence and NO code-deploy correlation = look UPSTREAM at the external API's QUOTA, not infra. The 2026-06-28 Google 504 cluster (06:20–11:40Z) AND the 4h geo "stall" were ONE event: Basic-Access developer-scope quota exhaustion (15k ops/day, one shared dev token) burned by the morning geo fan-out by ~11:32Z. FALSIFIED, explicitly: (a) Supabase swap/memory and (b) BUDGET_MS 680 — neither caused nor fixed the 504s (they ran 5.5h AFTER the BUDGET_MS deploy and stopped exactly when geo WRITES stopped, 3.5h BEFORE the Supabase resize). Read the REAL error bytes (e.errors[0]) before blaming infra; correlate the symptom's start/stop against the actual workload, not against whatever was deployed.
63 A backfill lap that throws OR fails to advance but lets the cron fire return HTTP 200 is a SILENT failure — geo was DEAD 4h under green 200s with the error masked as "[object Object]". Every drain fire must return ok:false/failed:N + console.error for ANY thrown/non-200 lap (ALL platforms); a dead/non-advancing lap can never read as a green fire. (LORAMER_GOOGLE_QUOTA_GUARD_V1 CHANGE 1.)
64 TWO completion authorities that can disagree are a stall trap: the sync_state cursor backfill_complete (writer) vs platform_connections.onboard_steps_done (drain). A stale done-flag over an INCOMPLETE cursor silently SKIPS a client forever (Woo Shelley: onboard ['woo'] done but cursor complete=false at 2018-12-13, owes to ~2015 — frozen ~12d; drain pending filter excludes her). The cursor must be the SINGLE completion authority; any path that re-opens a cursor to complete=false MUST clear that step key from onboard_steps_done.
65 Woo backfill "complete = one 21-day all-status-ZERO chunk" (woocommerce-backfill.ts) can FALSE-complete on any >21-day sales GAP mid-history — a quiet store stretch reads as history-start. When hardening woo completeness: probe the store's true oldest order, or require N consecutive zero chunks.
66 supabase-js .upsert(row) WITHOUT an explicit { onConflict } defaults its conflict target to the PRIMARY KEY. On a table whose real dedup key is a SECONDARY UNIQUE column (meta_tokens: PK=id + UNIQUE(user_email)), and where the PK is auto-generated (no id in the row), the upsert becomes an INSERT → it violates the secondary UNIQUE → 409, and if the returned error is discarded the write is a SILENT no-op that still looks successful. This bit the Meta callback: re-auth never rewrote the token (only the first-ever connect worked; the success redirect fired regardless), which broke the cote@ refresh. RULE: every upsert names its conflict target explicitly ({ onConflict: '<the-unique-column>' }) AND checks the returned error (fail loud — redirect/throw, never swallow, per L15). Gate-A a token/dedup upsert by reproducing the SECOND write to an existing key: buggy path 409s, fixed path UPDATES in place (id stable, 1 row). (LORAMER_META_CALLBACK_ONCONFLICT_V1, 2026-07-02.)
67 A Gate-A that checks only STATUS CODES can pass while the BEHAVIOR is broken — assert the behavior the gate exists to protect, not just 2xx/3xx. Origin: the 138a820 legacy-surface middleware silently broke the signup funnel two ways and that flight's Gate-A missed BOTH because it only read status codes: (a) it gated /agency + /business — the PRE-AUTH two-door signup pages — so unauthenticated new users were bounced to /login (the pages' content was never read → public marketing doors misclassified as "legacy tenant pages"); (b) it redirected /dashboard → -next BEFORE the /dashboard layout's enforceWelcomeGate could fire, so a fresh user reached the empty -next portfolio with NO account_type (Add-client 409s). The Gate-A even OBSERVED break (b) — /dashboard-next/clients returned 200 for a brand-new no-account_type user — and read it as "not over-blocked" instead of "onboarding didn't fire." RULE: for any gate/redirect/auth change, (1) READ what each matched path actually IS before gating it (public vs authed, data vs marketing), and (2) assert the POSITIVE behavior it must preserve — "a fresh user is REDIRECTED to /welcome", "the door RENDERS unauthenticated" — a bare 200 or 307 is necessary, NEVER sufficient. (LORAMER_SIGNUP_FUNNEL_FIX_V1, 2026-07-14.)
(2026-06-22) Product/line grain must reconcile to its account grain on the SAME revenue basis; re-capture history ONLY AFTER the basis fix ships (re-capturing before forces a second pass — violates "never twice").
